| int
| find_stack_direction ()
| {
|   static char *addr = 0;
|   auto char dummy;
|   if (addr == 0)
|     {
|       addr = &dummy;
|       return find_stack_direction ();
|     }
|   else
|     return (&dummy > addr) ? 1 : -1;
| }
| 
| int
| main ()
| {
|   return find_stack_direction () < 0;
| }
